      <article class="post type-post status-publish format-standard entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
         <!-- #BeginEditable "PageHeading" -->
         Historical Inflation 
						Rate
         <!-- #EndEditable -->
        </h1>
        <p class="entry-meta">
         <!-- #BeginEditable "article_date" -->
         <time class="entry-time" datetime="2015-06-18" itemprop="datePublished">
          June 18, 2015
         </time>
         <!-- #EndEditable -->
         by
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <!-- #BeginEditable "author" -->
          <a href="https://plus.google.com/114447364811707253880" rel="author">
           Tim McMahon
          </a>
          on
          <!-- #EndEditable -->
         </span>
         <span class="entry-comments-link">
          <a href="#respond">
           Leave a 
					Comment
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <!-- #BeginEditable "shareaholic" -->
        <div class="shareaholic-canvas" data-app="share_buttons" data-app-id="17774" data-link="http://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Rate/HistoricalInflation.aspx" data-summary="" data-title="Historical Inflation Rate">
        </div>
        <!-- #EndEditable -->
        <div class="ezAdsense adsense adsense-leadin" style="float: left; margin: 12px 25px 12px 12px;">
         <script async="" src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js">
         </script>
         <!-- ID 300x250 InPost - Image -->
         <ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-9339579720418175" data-ad-slot="3726141514" style="display: inline-block; width: 300px; height: 250px">
         </ins>
         <script>
          (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
         </script>
        </div>
        <!-- #BeginEditable "TopContent" -->
        <p>
         The
         <a href="#table">
          table below
         </a>
         provides the Historical U.S. Inflation 
							Rate data from 1914 to the Present. For a smaller table with just the 
							inflation rate data since the year 2000, see the
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Rate/CurrentInflation.asp">
          Current Inflation
         </a>
         page.
        </p>
        <p>
         The
         <strong>
          <em>
           Inflation rate
          </em>
         </strong>
         is 
							calculated from the Consumer Price Index (
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Consumer_Price_Index/CPI.asp">
          CPI-U
         </a>
         ) which 
							is compiled by the
         <a href="http://stats.bls.gov/news.release/cpi.t01.htm" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          U.S. Bureau of Labor Statistics
         </a>
         and is based upon a 1982-84 Base of 100. 
							Would you like to know the
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/2010/07/21/real-definition-inflation/">
          real definition of inflation
         </a>
         or
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/inflation/inflation_articles/calculateinflation.asp">
          how to calculate inflation?
         </a>
         or the
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Rate/Monthly_Inflation.aspx">
          monthly
         </a>
         rather than annual inflation rate? To view the actual Consumer 
							Price Index data that this inflation data is calculated 
							from, go to the
         <a href="../Consumer_Price_Index/HistoricalCPI.aspx">
          Historical CPI table
         </a>
         .
         <span class="auto-style4">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span class="auto-style4">
          Note: Due to the width of 
							the table, this page is best viewed full screen or 
							as wide as possible.
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Historical Inflation" class="alignright" src="../images/Inflation-10017482.jpg" style="float: right; height: 149px;" width="321"/>
         To see an in depth view of the inflationary 
						makeup of each decade:
         <br/>
         |
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-consumer-price-index-decade-commentary/inflation-cpi-consumer-price-index-1913-1919/">
          1913-19
         </a>
         |
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-cpi-consumer-price-index-1920-1929/">
          1920-29
         </a>
         |
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-cpi-consumer-price-index-1930-1939/">
          1930-39
         </a>
         |
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-consumer-price-index-decade-commentary/inflation-cpi-consumer-price-index-1940-1949/">
          1940-49
         </a>
         |
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-cpi-consumer-price-index-1950-1959/">
          1950-59
         </a>
         |
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-cpi-consumer-price-index-1960-1969/">
          1960-69
         </a>
         |
							|
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-cpi-consumer-price-index-1970-1979/">
          1970-79
         </a>
         |
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-cpi-consumer-price-index-1980-1989/">
          1980-89
         </a>
         |
         <span class="auto-style3">
          <br/>
          Coming soon | 1990-99 | 2000-09 | 2010- Present |
          <br/>
          Jump to
          <a href="#BottomInflation">
           Bottom of InflationTable
          </a>
          or click "year" to reverse order. Click "Ave" to sort years 
					by Average Annual inflation rate rather than date (click again to reverse).
         </span>
         <span class="auto-style3">
          Blank Cells indicate that the data is not available because it has not been released by the Bureau of Labor Statistics yet.
         </span>
        </p>

             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              1.02 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              1.02 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              0.00 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              2.06 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              1.02 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              1.01 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              3.03 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              2.00 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              1.00 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              0.99 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              1.00 %
             </td>
             <td style="font-size:XX-Small;white-space:nowrap;">
              1.35 %
             </td>
            </tr>
           </table>
          </div>
         </div>
        </form>
        <p class="auto-style2">
         <a href="#table">
          Return to 
							Top of Table
         </a>
         <a name="BottomInflation">
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         A CPI of 195 indicates 95% inflation 
							since 1982*, the commonly quoted
         <strong>
          <em>
           inflation 
							rate
          </em>
         </strong>
         of say 3% is actually the change 
							in the Consumer Price Index from a year earlier.
        </p>
        <p>
         The "Annual" on this table is the Average 
							of the individual
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Rate/CurrentInflation.asp">
          Inflation
         </a>
         rates for that year. Caution, 
							you cannot just add the inflation rates from two consecutive 
							years or even average them to find the total inflation 
							between two dates. If you would like to calculate the 
							inflation rate between two dates you must base your 
							calculations on the actual CPI index or you can use 
							our handy easy to use
         <a href="../Inflation_Calculators/Cumulative_Inflation_Calculator.aspx">
          Inflation calculator
         </a>
         or you might prefer to use 
							our
         <a href="../Cost_of_Living/Cost_of_Living_Calculator.asp">
          Cost of Living Calculator
         </a>
         to compare the costs in 
							two cities.
        </p>
        <p>
         You can find links to Inflation and 
							Consumer Price Index data for other countries
         <a href="InternationalSites.asp">
          HERE
         </a>
         . A chart of
         <a href="../Inflation/DecadeInflation.asp">
          Inflation 
							by decade
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="../Inflation/AnnualInflation.asp">
          Annual Inflation
         </a>
         and
         <a href="ConfederateInflation.asp">
          Confederate Inflation
         </a>
         is also available. Menu navigation is available on every page. We have
         <a href="../Articles.asp">
          a complete listing of all 
							of our Articles
         </a>
         on inflation, including Inflation
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/2010/07/21/real-definition-inflation/">
          Definitions
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://inflationdata.com/articles/2009/11/25/which-is-better-high-or-low-inflation/">
          Which is better High or Low Inflation
         </a>
         , and
         <a href="../Inflation_Articles/CalculateInflation.asp">
          How to Calculate Inflation
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="Historical_Oil_Prices_Chart.asp">
          Inflation 
							Adjusted Oil Prices (Chart)
         </a>
         and
         <a href="Historical_Oil_Prices_Table.asp">
          Inflation 
							Adjusted Oil Prices (table)
         </a>
         and a
         <a href="Monthly_Inflation.aspx">
          Monthly Inflation Rate 
							Table
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         <font size="2">
          * Actually the index applies to an 
							average of 1982-1984 so there is no specific date 
							when the index was exactly 100. (If you check the 
							chart
          <a href="../Consumer_Price_Index/HistoricalCPI.aspx">
           here
          </a>
          you will see it was somewhere between July 
							and August of 1983. But the reference year is 
							commonly referred to as 1982.)
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font size="2">
          You might also be interested in the 
							wide variety of articles on our sister site Financial 
							Trend Forecaster a complete list of 
							the articles on Financial Trend Forecaster is at the
          <a href="http://fintrend.com/sitemap/" rel="nofollow">
           FTF Article 
							Archives
          </a>
          .
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         To calculate inflation from a month and year to a 
							later month and year, Try our
         <a href="../Inflation_Calculators/Cumulative_Inflation_Calculator.aspx">
          Inflation calculator
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Image courtesy of jscreationzs / FreeDigitalPhotos.net
        </p>
